PHPMailer -\/ PHP email creation and transport class.

Brent R. Matzelle (original founder) 
\end{DoxyAuthor}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{addAttachment()}{addAttachment()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily add\+Attachment (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$path,  }\item[{}]{\$name = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$encoding = {\ttfamily self\+:\+:ENCODING\+\_\+BASE64},  }\item[{}]{\$type = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$disposition = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}attachment\textquotesingle{}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Add an attachment from a path on the filesystem. Never use a user-\/supplied path to a file! Returns false if the file could not be found or read. Explicitly {\itshape does not} support passing URLs; PHPMailer is not an HTTP client. If you need to do that, fetch the resource yourself and pass it in via a local file or string.

\hline

string & {\em \$disposition} & Disposition to use\\

\Hypertarget{class_p_h_p_mailer_1_1_p_h_p_mailer_1_1_p_h_p_mailer_ab9dec7369dc3dcc3c07176791a29d9e6}\label{class_p_h_p_mailer_1_1_p_h_p_mailer_1_1_p_h_p_mailer_ab9dec7369dc3dcc3c07176791a29d9e6} 
\index{PHPMailer@{PHPMailer}!addEmbeddedImage@{addEmbeddedImage}}
\index{addEmbeddedImage@{addEmbeddedImage}!PHPMailer@{PHPMailer}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{addEmbeddedImage()}{addEmbeddedImage()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily add\+Embedded\+Image (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$path,  }\item[{}]{\$cid,  }\item[{}]{\$name = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$encoding = {\ttfamily self\+:\+:ENCODING\+\_\+BASE64},  }\item[{}]{\$type = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$disposition = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}inline\textquotesingle{}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Add an embedded (inline) attachment from a file. This can include images, sounds, and just about any other document type. These differ from \textquotesingle{}regular\textquotesingle{} attachments in that they are intended to be displayed inline with the message, not just attached for download. This is used in HTML messages that embed the images the HTML refers to using the {\ttfamily \$cid} value in {\ttfamily img} tags, for example {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}img src="{}cid\+:mylogo"{}\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}}. Never use a user-\/supplied path to a file!


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
string & {\em \$path} & Path to the attachment \\
\hline
string & {\em \$cid} & Content ID of the attachment; Use this to reference the content when using an embedded image in HTML \\
\hline
string & {\em \$name} & Overrides the attachment filename \\
\hline
string & {\em \$encoding} & File encoding (see \$\+Encoding) defaults to {\ttfamily base64} \\
\hline
string & {\em \$type} & File MIME type (by default mapped from the {\ttfamily \$path} filename\textquotesingle{}s extension) \\
\hline
string & {\em \$disposition} & Disposition to use\+: {\ttfamily inline} (default) or {\ttfamily attachment} (unlikely you want this – \{\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}
{\ttfamily add\+Attachment()}\} instead)
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

bool True on successfully adding an attachment 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{PHPMailer@{PHPMailer}!addOrEnqueueAnAddress@{addOrEnqueueAnAddress}}
\index{addOrEnqueueAnAddress@{addOrEnqueueAnAddress}!PHPMailer@{PHPMailer}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{addOrEnqueueAnAddress()}{addOrEnqueueAnAddress()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily add\+Or\+Enqueue\+An\+Address (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$kind,  }\item[{}]{\$address,  }\item[{}]{\$name }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}

Add an address to one of the recipient arrays or to the Reply\+To array. Because PHPMailer can\textquotesingle{}t validate addresses with an IDN without knowing the PHPMailer\+::\$\+Char\+Set (that can still be modified after calling this function), addition of such addresses is delayed until send(). Addresses that have been added already return false, but do not throw exceptions.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
string & {\em \$kind} & One of \textquotesingle{}to\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}cc\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}bcc\textquotesingle{}, or \textquotesingle{}Reply\+To\textquotesingle{} \\
\hline
string & {\em \$address} & The email address \\
\hline
string & {\em \$name} & An optional username associated with the address\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyExceptions}{Exceptions}
{\em Exception} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyExceptions}

bool true on success, false if address already used or invalid in some way 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Add an address to one of the recipient arrays or to the Reply\+To array. Because PHPMailer can\textquotesingle{}t validate addresses with an IDN without knowing the PHPMailer\+::\$\+Char\+Set (that can still be modified after calling this function), addition of such addresses is delayed until send(). Addresses that have been added already return false, but do not throw exceptions.

Add an embedded stringified attachment. This can include images, sounds, and just about any other document type. If your filename doesn\textquotesingle{}t contain an extension, be sure to set the \$type to an appropriate MIME type.

\hline
string & {\em \$encoding} & File encoding (see \$\+Encoding), defaults to \textquotesingle{}base64\textquotesingle{} \\
\hline
string & {\em \$type} & MIME type -\/ will be used in preference to any automatically derived type \\
\hline
string & {\em \$disposition} & Disposition to use\\

Generate a DKIM canonicalization body. Uses the \textquotesingle{}simple\textquotesingle{} algorithm from RFC6376 section 3.\+4.\+3. Canonicalized bodies should {\itshape always} use CRLF, regardless of mailer setting.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{isShellSafe()}{isShellSafe()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static is\+Shell\+Safe (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$string }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}, {\ttfamily [protected]}}

Fix CVE-\/2016-\/10033 and CVE-\/2016-\/10045 by disallowing potentially unsafe shell characters. Note that escapeshellarg and escapeshellcmd are inadequate for our purposes, especially on Windows.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}
\href{https://github.com/PHPMailer/PHPMailer/issues/924}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/\+PHPMailer/\+PHPMailer/issues/924}} CVE-\/2016-\/10045 bug report
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
string & {\em \$string} & The string to be validated\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
bool 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\Hypertarget{class_p_h_p_mailer_1_1_p_h_p_mailer_1_1_p_h_p_mailer_aa9e20d8f3d4181d188ee1a4d43e4737e}\label{class_p_h_p_mailer_1_1_p_h_p_mailer_1_1_p_h_p_mailer_aa9e20d8f3d4181d188ee1a4d43e4737e} 
\index{PHPMailer@{PHPMailer}!isShellSafe@{isShellSafe}}
\index{isShellSafe@{isShellSafe}!PHPMailer@{PHPMailer}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{isShellSafe()}{isShellSafe()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static is\+Shell\+Safe (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$string }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}, {\ttfamily [protected]}}

Fix CVE-\/2016-\/10033 and CVE-\/2016-\/10045 by disallowing potentially unsafe shell characters. Note that escapeshellarg and escapeshellcmd are inadequate for our purposes, especially on Windows.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}
\href{https://github.com/PHPMailer/PHPMailer/issues/924}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/\+PHPMailer/\+PHPMailer/issues/924}} CVE-\/2016-\/10045 bug report
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\Hypertarget{class_p_h_p_mailer_1_1_p_h_p_mailer_1_1_p_h_p_mailer_a6f48abba605717de6ac66ea2cceef1b1}\label{class_p_h_p_mailer_1_1_p_h_p_mailer_1_1_p_h_p_mailer_a6f48abba605717de6ac66ea2cceef1b1} 
\index{PHPMailer@{PHPMailer}!msgHTML@{msgHTML}}
\index{msgHTML@{msgHTML}!PHPMailer@{PHPMailer}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{msgHTML()}{msgHTML()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily msg\+HTML (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$message,  }\item[{}]{\$basedir = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$advanced = {\ttfamily false} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Create a message body from an HTML string. Automatically inlines images and creates a plain-\/text version by converting the HTML, overwriting any existing values in Body and Alt\+Body. Do not source \$message content from user input! \$basedir is prepended when handling relative URLs, e.\+g.  and must not be empty will look for an image file in \$basedir/images/a.png and convert it to inline. If you don\textquotesingle{}t provide a \$basedir, relative paths will be left untouched (and thus probably break in email) Converts data-\/uri images into embedded attachments. If you don\textquotesingle{}t want to apply these transformations to your HTML, just set Body and Alt\+Body directly.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
string & {\em \$message} & HTML message string \\
\hline
string & {\em \$basedir} & Absolute path to a base directory to prepend to relative paths to images \\
\hline
bool | callable & {\em \$advanced} & Whether to use the internal HTML to text converter or your own custom converter \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
string The transformed message body
\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxyExceptions}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{parseAddresses()}{parseAddresses()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static parse\+Addresses (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$addrstr,  }\item[{}]{\$useimap = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{}]{\$charset = {\ttfamily self\+:\+:CHARSET\+\_\+ISO88591} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Parse and validate a string containing one or more RFC822-\/style comma-\/separated email addresses of the form "{}display name $<$address$>$"{} into an array of name/address pairs. Uses the imap\+\_\+rfc822\+\_\+parse\+\_\+adrlist function if the IMAP extension is available. Note that quotes in the name part are removed.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}
\href{http://www.andrew.cmu.edu/user/agreen1/testing/mrbs/web/Mail/RFC822.php}{\texttt{ http\+://www.\+andrew.\+cmu.\+edu/user/agreen1/testing/mrbs/web/\+Mail/\+RFC822.\+php}} A more careful implementation
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\Hypertarget{class_p_h_p_mailer_1_1_p_h_p_mailer_1_1_p_h_p_mailer_a53f031a9823e893efcae14422999619b}\label{class_p_h_p_mailer_1_1_p_h_p_mailer_1_1_p_h_p_mailer_a53f031a9823e893efcae14422999619b} 
\index{PHPMailer@{PHPMailer}!punyencodeAddress@{punyencodeAddress}}
\index{punyencodeAddress@{punyencodeAddress}!PHPMailer@{PHPMailer}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{punyencodeAddress()}{punyencodeAddress()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily punyencode\+Address (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$address }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Converts IDN in given email address to its ASCII form, also known as punycode, if possible. Important\+: Address must be passed in same encoding as currently set in PHPMailer\+::\$\+Char\+Set. This function silently returns unmodified address if\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item No conversion is necessary (i.\+e. domain name is not an IDN, or is already in ASCII form)
\item Conversion to punycode is impossible (e.\+g. required PHP functions are not available) or fails for any reason (e.\+g. domain contains characters not allowed in an IDN).
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}
PHPMailer\+::\$\+Char\+Set
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
string & {\em \$address} & The email address to convert\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
string The encoded address in ASCII form 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\Hypertarget{class_p_h_p_mailer_1_1_p_h_p_mailer_1_1_p_h_p_mailer_a53f031a9823e893efcae14422999619b}\label{class_p_h_p_mailer_1_1_p_h_p_mailer_1_1_p_h_p_mailer_a53f031a9823e893efcae14422999619b} 
\index{PHPMailer@{PHPMailer}!punyencodeAddress@{punyencodeAddress}}
\index{punyencodeAddress@{punyencodeAddress}!PHPMailer@{PHPMailer}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{punyencodeAddress()}{punyencodeAddress()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily punyencode\+Address (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$address }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Converts IDN in given email address to its ASCII form, also known as punycode, if possible. Important\+: Address must be passed in same encoding as currently set in PHPMailer\+::\$\+Char\+Set. This function silently returns unmodified address if\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item No conversion is necessary (i.\+e. domain name is not an IDN, or is already in ASCII form)
\item Conversion to punycode is impossible (e.\+g. required PHP functions are not available) or fails for any reason (e.\+g. domain contains characters not allowed in an IDN).
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\index{setBoundaries@{setBoundaries}!PHPMailer@{PHPMailer}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setBoundaries()}{setBoundaries()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily set\+Boundaries (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Set the boundaries to use for delimiting MIME parts. If you override this, ensure you set all 3 boundaries to unique values. The default boundaries include a "{}=\+\_\+"{} sequence which cannot occur in quoted-\/printable bodies, as suggested by \href{https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc2045\#section-6.7}{\texttt{ https\+://www.\+rfc-\/editor.\+org/rfc/rfc2045\#section-\/6.\+7}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
void 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setWordWrap()}{setWordWrap()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily set\+Word\+Wrap (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Apply word wrapping to the message body. Wraps the message body to the number of chars set in the Word\+Wrap property. You should only do this to plain-\/text bodies as wrapping HTML tags may break them. This is called automatically by create\+Body(), so you don\textquotesingle{}t need to call it yourself. \Hypertarget{class_p_h_p_mailer_1_1_p_h_p_mailer_1_1_p_h_p_mailer_ab3b2787c3d322ed943f863c6bf2e4bc8}\label{class_p_h_p_mailer_1_1_p_h_p_mailer_1_1_p_h_p_mailer_ab3b2787c3d322ed943f863c6bf2e4bc8}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily set\+Word\+Wrap (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Apply word wrapping to the message body. Wraps the message body to the number of chars set in the Word\+Wrap property. You should only do this to plain-\/text bodies as wrapping HTML tags may break them. This is called automatically by create\+Body(), so you don\textquotesingle{}t need to call it yourself. \Hypertarget{class_p_h_p_mailer_1_1_p_h_p_mailer_1_1_p_h_p_mailer_ade9654aa4a545955b7058c18f837db8f}\label{class_p_h_p_mailer_1_1_p_h_p_mailer_1_1_p_h_p_mailer_ade9654aa4a545955b7058c18f837db8f}

\Hypertarget{class_p_h_p_mailer_1_1_p_h_p_mailer_1_1_p_h_p_mailer_ab1751a18a24757fee7043fa3b055eb03}\label{class_p_h_p_mailer_1_1_p_h_p_mailer_1_1_p_h_p_mailer_ab1751a18a24757fee7043fa3b055eb03} 
\index{PHPMailer@{PHPMailer}!validateAddress@{validateAddress}}
\index{validateAddress@{validateAddress}!PHPMailer@{PHPMailer}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{validateAddress()}{validateAddress()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static validate\+Address (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$address,  }\item[{}]{\$patternselect = {\ttfamily null} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Check that a string looks like an email address. Validation patterns supported\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily auto} Pick best pattern automatically;
\item {\ttfamily pcre8} Use the squiloople.\+com pattern, requires PCRE \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 8.\+0;
\item {\ttfamily pcre} Use old PCRE implementation;
\item {\ttfamily php} Use PHP built-\/in FILTER\+\_\+\+VALIDATE\+\_\+\+EMAIL;
\item {\ttfamily html5} Use the pattern given by the HTML5 spec for \textquotesingle{}email\textquotesingle{} type form input elements.
\item {\ttfamily noregex} Don\textquotesingle{}t use a regex\+: super fast, really dumb. Alternatively you may pass in a callable to inject your own validator, for example\+:
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{PHPMailer::validateAddress(\textcolor{stringliteral}{'user@example.com'},\ \textcolor{keyword}{function}(\$address)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ (strpos(\$address,\ \textcolor{charliteral}{'@'})\ !==\ \textcolor{keyword}{false});}
\DoxyCodeLine{\});}

\end{DoxyCode}


You can also set the PHPMailer\+::\$validator static to a callable, allowing built-\/in methods to use your validator.

string & {\em \$address} & The email address to check \\
\hline
string | callable & {\em \$patternselect} & Which pattern to use\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

bool 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Word-\/wrap message. For use with mailers that do not automatically perform wrapping and for quoted-\/printable encoded messages. Original written by philippe.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
string & {\em \$message} & The message to wrap \\
\hline
int & {\em \$length} & The line length to wrap to \\
\hline
bool & {\em \$qp\+\_\+mode} & Whether to run in Quoted-\/\+Printable mode\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
string 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{PHPMailer@{PHPMailer}!\$dsn@{\$dsn}}
\index{\$dsn@{\$dsn}!PHPMailer@{PHPMailer}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{\$dsn}{\$dsn}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \$dsn = \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}}

Comma separated list of DSN notifications \textquotesingle{}NEVER\textquotesingle{} under no circumstances a DSN must be returned to the sender. If you use NEVER all other notifications will be ignored. \textquotesingle{}SUCCESS\textquotesingle{} will notify you when your mail has arrived at its destination. \textquotesingle{}FAILURE\textquotesingle{} will arrive if an error occurred during delivery. \textquotesingle{}DELAY\textquotesingle{} will notify you if there is an unusual delay in delivery, but the actual delivery\textquotesingle{}s outcome (success or failure) is not yet decided.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}
\href{https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc3461}{\texttt{ https\+://tools.\+ietf.\+org/html/rfc3461}} See section 4.\+1 for more information about NOTIFY 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
